country_event = { 
	id = canarias.2
	title = "canarias.2EVTNAME"
	desc = "canarias.2EVTDESC"
	picture = SIEGE_eventPicture
	trigger = { 
		PAP = { 
			has_country_flag = asked_canarias_mission_pap
		}
		NOT = { 
			CNA = { 
				has_country_flag = canarias_mission_received
			}
		}
		NOT = { 
			CNA = { 
				has_country_flag = canarias_conquista_arrived
			}
		}
		religion = catholic
		AND = { 
			OR = { 
				is_subject = no
				is_subject_of_type = tributary_state

			}
		}
		OR = { 
			capital_scope = { 
				OR = { 
					region = aragon_region
					region = castille_region
					region = leon_region
					region = andalucia_region
					region = portugal_region
				}
			}
			AND = { 
				tag = FRA
				has_global_flag = hundred_years_war_FRA_win
				NOT = { 
					is_year = 1380
				}
			}
			AND = { 
				capital_scope = { 
					superregion = italy_superregion
				}
				monthly_income = 10
				num_of_ports = 1
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		years = 10
		modifier = { 
			factor = 0.25
			owns = 333

			factor = 0.25
			tag = POR
			NOT = { 
				has_country_flag = declined_canarias_mission
			}
		}
		modifier = { 
			factor = 0.25
			OR = { 
				tag = GEN
				tag = VEN
			}
			NOT = { 
				has_country_flag = declined_canarias_mission
			}
		}
		modifier = { 
			factor = 0.25

country_event = { 
	id = canarias.3
	title = "canarias.3EVTNAME"
	desc = "canarias.3EVTDESC"
	picture = SIEGE_eventPicture
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { 
		name = "canarias.3a"
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 50
		}
		random_owned_province = { 
			limit = { 
				NOT = { 
					religion = catholic
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = { 
				name = heretic_missionary
				duration = 1825
			}
			set_province_flag = canarias_missionary_flag
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "canarias.3b"
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 50
		}
		FROM = { 
			country_event = { 
				id = canarias.28
				days = 30
				random = 15
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = { 
	id = canarias.10
	title = "canarias.10EVTNAME"
	desc = "canarias.10EVTDESC"
	picture = SIEGE_eventPicture
	is_triggered_only = yes
	major = yes
	trigger = { 
		is_capital = yes
		owned_by = CNA
		controlled_by = REB
		owner = { 
			has_country_flag = canarias_conquista_arrived
			NOT = { 
				has_country_flag = conquista_successful
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "canarias.10a"
		random_country = { 
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = canarias_conquista
			}
			country_event = { 
				id = canarias.11
				days = 30
				random = 15
			}
		}
		owner = { 
			change_religion = catholic
			change_government = monarchy
			add_government_reform = Pol_Succession1
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					custom_trigger_tooltip = { 
						tooltip = is_monarchy_tt
						OR = { 
							government = monarchy
							government = has_harem
						}
					}
					is_variable_equal = { 
						which = grj
						value = 4
					}
					OR = { 
						NOT = { 
							religion_group = muslim
						}
						culture_group = tartar_group
						culture_group = old_turkic
						culture_group = altaic
						primary_culture = turkish
					}
					NOT = { 
						religion_group = christian
					}
					NOT = { 
						culture_group = japanese_g
					}
				}
				add_government_reform = Pol_Family4
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					custom_trigger_tooltip = { 
						tooltip = is_monarchy_tt
						OR = { 
							government = monarchy
							government = has_harem
						}
					}
					is_variable_equal = { 
						which = grj
						value = 4
					}
					religion_group = muslim
					NOT = { 
						culture_group = tartar_group
					}
					NOT = { 
						culture_group = old_turkic
					}
					NOT = { 
						culture_group = altaic
					}
					NOT = { 
						primary_culture = turkish
					}
				}
				add_government_reform = Pol_Family3
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					custom_trigger_tooltip = { 
						tooltip = is_monarchy_tt
						OR = { 
							government = monarchy
							government = has_harem
						}
					}
					OR = { 
						is_variable_equal = { 
							which = grj
							value = 1
						}
						religion_group = muslim
					}
					NOT = { 
						primary_culture = turkish
					}
				}
				add_government_reform = Pol_Family2
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					custom_trigger_tooltip = { 
						tooltip = is_monarchy_tt
						OR = { 
							government = monarchy
							government = has_harem
						}
					}
					is_tribal = no
				}
				add_government_reform = Pol_Family1
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					is_variable_equal = { 
						which = gri
						value = 0
					}
				}
				add_government_reform = Pol_Nobility1
			}
			else_if = {

						value = 1

			if = {

					is_variable_equal = { 
						which = gqr
						value = 0

				add_government_reform = Pol_Structure1

			add_government_reform = Pol_Nobility1

					}
					set_variable = { 
						which = ahf
						value = 0
					}
				}
				else = {

				}
			}
			tooltip = { 
				add_stability = -3
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					is_emperor_of_china = yes
				}
				add_mandate = -15
			}
			disband_rebels = catholic_rebels
			every_owned_province = { 
				limit = { 
					controlled_by = REB
				}
				change_controller = CNA
			}
		}
	}

	desc = "canarias.32EVTDESC"
	picture = SIEGE_eventPicture
	trigger = { 
		tag = CNA
		has_country_flag = canarias_mission_received
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		years = 50
	}
	option = { 
		name = "canarias.32a"
		clr_country_flag = canarias_mission_received
		every_owned_province = { 
			limit = { 
				has_province_modifier = heretic_missionary
			}
			remove_province_modifier = heretic_missionary
		}
		every_country = { 
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = canarias_mission_send
			}
			set_country_flag = declined_canarias_mission
			clr_country_flag = canarias_mission_send
			clr_country_flag = canarias_bribe_100
			clr_country_flag = canarias_bribe_25
			clr_country_flag = canarias_bribe_50
			remove_country_modifier = canarias_mission_modifier
			country_event = { 
				id = canarias.35
				days = 30
				random = 15
			}
		}
	}
}

	option = { 
		name = "canarias.40a"
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 50
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0
				religion = catholic
			}
		}
		free_vassal = CNA
		366 = { 
			add_claim = ROOT
		}
		2751 = { 
			add_claim = ROOT
		}
		FROM = { 
			country_event = { 
				id = canarias.41
				days = 30
				random = 15
			}
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = "canarias.40b"
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 50
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0
				NOT = { 
					religion_group = christian
				}
			}
		}
		add_prestige = -5
		FROM = { 
			country_event = { 
				id = canarias.42
				days = 30
				random = 15
			}
		}
	}
}
